<div class="wp-block-stackable-heading stk-block-heading stk-block-heading--v2 stk-block stk-fbf4c84" id="our-core-values-form-the-foundation-of-how-br-we-perform-work-and-conduct-ourselves" data-block-id="fbf4c84"><h2 class="stk-block-heading__text has-text-color">Our core values form the foundation of how<br>we perform work and conduct ourselves.</h2></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-38588da" id="our-core-values-form-the-foundation-of-how-br-we-perform-work-and-conduct-ourselves" data-block-id="38588da"><p class="stk-block-text__text">We are&nbsp;<strong>People First</strong>.</p></div>



<div class="wp-block-stackable-text stk-block-text stk-block stk-bb4277d" id="our-core-values-form-the-foundation-of-how-br-we-perform-work-and-conduct-ourselves" data-block-id="bb4277d"><p class="stk-block-text__text">We believe&nbsp;<strong>Bright Future</strong>&nbsp;is possible by being optimistic, encouraging and positive.</p></div>
